       <div class="toc-section"> <h5><a href="/sandbox/nTR8nJOW/realm/X7li5Fcx">The Lands of Vo'il</a></h5> <p> <blockquote>A charismatic leader has united Vo'il’s disparate thieves’ guilds into one organisation. Bishop Galicius wants this figurehead removed lest they threaten the status quo.</blockquote> </p>  <div class="toc-subsection">  <div class="toc-column"> <h6>Regions</h6> <ul>  <li><a
